function ez_isclean( data ) {
    if (typeof data === 'undefined') { data = document.URL; }
    var re = /(([^<>()[\]\\.,;:\s@\"]+(\.[^<>()[\]\\.,;:\s@\"]+)*)|(\".+\"))(@|%2540|%40)((\[[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\])|(([a-zA-Z\-0-9]+\.)+[a-zA-Z]{2,}))/;
    var isClean = !re.test(data);
    return isClean;
}

var ez_queue = new Array();
function sort_queue(a, b)
{
  if( a.priority < b.priority ) return -1;
  else if( a.priority == b.priority ) return 0;
  else return 1;
}
function execute_ez_queue()
{
  ez_queue.sort( sort_queue );

  for( var i in ez_queue )
  {
        if(typeof ez_queue[i].method != "undefined")
        {
            try{
                ez_queue[i].method.call( null );
            }
            catch (err) {

            }
        }
  }
}

    if(ez_isclean() && d instanceof Array) {
        if(typeof ezstandalone !== 'undefined' && typeof ezstandalone.selectedPlaceholders !== 'undefined' && ezstandalone.selectedPlaceholders[d[3]] === true) {
            return "1+1";
        }
        ez_ad_units[ez_ad_units.length] = d;

        return ezcmd;
    }

    return "1+1";
}
function in_array(needle, haystack) {
    var length = haystack.length;
    for(var i = 0; i < length; i++) {
        if(haystack[i] == needle) return true;
    }
    return false;
}

                        <header class="td-post-title">
                            <h1 class="entry-title">Libyan Army attacks Turkeys main base in Libya</h1>

                            

                            <div class="td-module-meta-info">
                                <div class="td-post-author-name"><div class="td-author-by">By</div> <a href="https://www.almasdarnews.com/article/author/dfroberg/">News Desk</a><div class="td-author-line"> - </div> </div>                                <span class="td-post-date"><time class="entry-date updated td-module-date" datetime="2020-04-26T15:01:50+00:00">2020-04-26</time></span>                                                                <div class="td-post-comments"><a href="https://www.almasdarnews.com/article/libyan-army-attacks-turkeys-main-base-in-libya/#respond"><i class="td-icon-comments"></i>0</a></div>                            </div>

                        </header>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div> <!-- /.td-pb-row -->

            <div class="td-pb-row">
                                            <div class="td-pb-span8 td-main-content" role="main">
                                <div class="td-ss-main-content">
                                            

        <div class="td-post-content">
            <div class="td-post-featured-image"><a href="https://www.almasdarnews.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/11/LNA-tank-in-Benghazi.jpg" data-caption=""><img width="890" height="516" class="ezlazyload entry-thumb td-modal-image" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns%3D%22http%3A%2F%2Fwww.w3.org%2F2000%2Fsvg%22%20width%3D%22890%22%20height%3D%22516%22%3E%3C%2Fsvg%3E" sizes="(max-width: 890px) 100vw, 890px" alt="" title="" ezimgfmt="rs rscb16 src ng ngcb16 srcset" data-ezsrc="https://www.almasdarnews.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/11/LNA-tank-in-Benghazi-890x516.jpg" data-ezsrcset="https://www.almasdarnews.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/11/LNA-tank-in-Benghazi-890x516.jpg 890w,https://www.almasdarnews.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/11/LNA-tank-in-Benghazi-768x445.jpg 768w,https://www.almasdarnews.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/11/LNA-tank-in-Benghazi-696x403.jpg 696w,https://www.almasdarnews.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/11/LNA-tank-in-Benghazi-1392x807.jpg 1392w,https://www.almasdarnews.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/11/LNA-tank-in-Benghazi-664x385.jpg 664w,https://www.almasdarnews.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/11/LNA-tank-in-Benghazi-1068x619.jpg 1068w,https://www.almasdarnews.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/11/LNA-tank-in-Benghazi-725x420.jpg 725w,https://www.almasdarnews.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/11/LNA-tank-in-Benghazi-1450x840.jpg 1450w,https://www.almasdarnews.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/11/LNA-tank-in-Benghazi-1920x1113.jpg 1920w,https://www.almasdarnews.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/11/LNA-tank-in-Benghazi-95x55.jpg 95w,https://www.almasdarnews.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/11/LNA-tank-in-Benghazi-580x336.jpg 580w,https://www.almasdarnews.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/11/LNA-tank-in-Benghazi-1049x608.jpg 1049w,https://www.almasdarnews.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/11/LNA-tank-in-Benghazi.jpg 2000w"></a></div>
            <div class="td-a-rec td-a-rec-id-content_top  td_uid_4_5ea6a14a3714e_rand td_block_template_1">
<style>
/* custom css */
.td_uid_4_5ea6a14a3714e_rand.td-a-rec-img {
				    text-align: left;
				}
				.td_uid_4_5ea6a14a3714e_rand.td-a-rec-img img {
                    margin: 0 auto 0 0;
                }
</style><!-- Ezoic - under_page_title 108 - under_page_title -->
<span id="ezoic-pub-ad-placeholder-108"></span><!-- placeholder 108 blocked.  Reason : inactive -->
<!-- End Ezoic - under_page_title 108 - under_page_title --></div><p><span id="ezoic-pub-ad-placeholder-133" class="ezoic-adpicker-ad"></span><span id="ezoic-pub-ad-placeholder-138" class="ezoic-adpicker-ad"></span>BEIRUT, LEBANON (2:45 P.M.)  The Libyan National Army (LNA) launched a heavy attack on the Mitiga Airbase in Tripoli on Sunday, targeting several sites inside this strategic installation that houses several Turkish military personnel.</p>
<p>According to a field report from Tripoli, the LNA heavily targeted the Mitiga Airbase with artillery shells and rockets, causing a number of explosions that could be heard throughout the capital.</p><div class="td-a-rec td-a-rec-id-content_inlineright  td_uid_3_5ea6a14a36fe5_rand td_block_template_1">
<style>
/* custom css */
.td_uid_3_5ea6a14a36fe5_rand.td-a-rec-img {
				    text-align: left;
				}
				.td_uid_3_5ea6a14a36fe5_rand.td-a-rec-img img {
                    margin: 0 auto 0 0;
                }
</style><!-- Ezoic - under_second_paragraph 110 - under_second_paragraph -->
<span id="ezoic-pub-ad-placeholder-110"></span><!-- placeholder 110 blocked.  Reason : inactive -->
<!-- End Ezoic - under_second_paragraph 110 - under_second_paragraph --></div>
<p><span id="ezoic-pub-ad-placeholder-134" class="ezoic-adpicker-ad"></span><span id="ezoic-pub-ad-placeholder-139" class="ezoic-adpicker-ad"></span>The Haftar terrorist militias continue to bomb the Grad rockets at Mitiga Airport and the residential neighborhoods in its vicinity, the Government of National Accord (GNA) forces announced this afternoon.</p>
<p>The Mitiga Airbase is Turkeys main base in Libya, as it not only houses their soldiers, but also their military equipment.</p>
<p><span id="ezoic-pub-ad-placeholder-136" class="ezoic-adpicker-ad"></span><span style='display:block !important;float:none;margin-bottom:15px !important;margin-left:0px !important;margin-right:0px !important;margin-top:15px !important;min-height:250px;min-width:300px;text-align:center !important;' class='ezoic-ad medrectangle-4 adtester-container adtester-container-136' data-ez-name='almasdarnews_com-medrectangle-4'><span id='div-gpt-ad-almasdarnews_com-medrectangle-4-0' ezaw='300' ezah='250' style='position:relative;z-index:0;display:inline-block;min-height:250px;min-width:300px;' class='ezoic-ad ezoic-adl'><script data-ezscrex='false' data-cfasync='false' type='text/javascript' style='display:none;'>eval(ez_write_tag([[300,250],'almasdarnews_com-medrectangle-4','ezslot_10',136,'0','0']));</script></span></span><span id="ezoic-pub-ad-placeholder-140" class="ezoic-adpicker-ad"></span>This latest development comes at a time when the fighting between the GNA and LNA forces are at their most violent and intense.</p>
<p>In an effort to calm the situation, the European Union recently launched a new initiative in the Mediterranean Sea called IRINI, which will focus on ensuring the implementation of the international arms embargo on Libya.</p>
<p>The GNA has already criticized this move by the European Union, as they view it as an attempt to prevent Turkish shipments to Tripoli.<span id="ezoic-pub-ad-placeholder-111" class="ezoic-adpicker-ad"></span><span style='display:block !important;float:none;margin-bottom:15px !important;margin-left:0px !important;margin-right:0px !important;margin-top:15px !important;min-height:250px;min-width:250px;text-align:center !important;' class='ezoic-ad box-4 adtester-container adtester-container-111' data-ez-name='almasdarnews_com-box-4'><span id='div-gpt-ad-almasdarnews_com-box-4-0' ezaw='250' ezah='250' style='position:relative;z-index:0;display:inline-block;min-height:250px;min-width:250px;' class='ezoic-ad ezoic-adl'><script data-ezscrex='false' data-cfasync='false' type='text/javascript' style='display:none;'>eval(ez_write_tag([[250,250],'almasdarnews_com-box-4','ezslot_0',111,'0','0']));</script></span></span></p>
		<div class="wpcnt"><span id="ezoic-pub-ad-placeholder-130" class="ezoic-adpicker-ad"></span>
			<div class="wpa">
				<span class="wpa-about">Advertisements</span>

	</div> <!-- ./td-related-span4 --></div><!--./row-fluid--></div><div class="td-next-prev-wrap"><a href="#" class="td-ajax-prev-page ajax-page-disabled" id="prev-page-td_uid_6_5ea6a14a37750" data-td_block_id="td_uid_6_5ea6a14a37750"><i class="td-icon-font td-icon-menu-left"></i></a><a href="#" class="td-ajax-next-page" id="next-page-td_uid_6_5ea6a14a37750" data-td_block_id="td_uid_6_5ea6a14a37750"><i class="td-icon-font td-icon-menu-right"></i></a><span id="ezoic-pub-ad-placeholder-115" class="ezoic-adpicker-ad"></span><span style='display:block !important;float:none;margin-bottom:15px !important;margin-left:0px !important;margin-right:0px !important;margin-top:15px !important;min-height:480px;min-width:100%;text-align:center !important;' class='ezoic-ad nativedouble-1 adtester-container adtester-container-115' data-ez-name='almasdarnews_com-nativedouble-1'><div class="OUTBRAIN" data-src="http://outbrain.ezoic.net/default/?variant=187524_1_115_100x480" data-widget-id="AR_1" data-ob-template="ezoic" data-external-id="187524_1_115_100x480" data-ob-srcUrl="http://outbrain.ezoic.net/"></div>
<script type="text/ez-screx" async="async" src="https://www.almasdarnews.com/ezossp/unknown/widgets.outbrain.com/outbrain.js?screx=1&sxcb=16a"></script></span></div></div> <!-- ./block -->	<div class="comments-note" id="comments-note">
		<div class="vc_row wpb_row td-pb-row"><div class="wpb_column vc_column_container td-pb-span8"><div class="vc_column-inner "><div class="wpb_wrapper"><div class="vc_message_box vc_message_box-standard vc_message_box-rounded vc_color-info"><div class="vc_message_box-icon"><i class="fas fa-info-circle"></i></div><p><strong>Notice:</strong> All comments represent the view of the commenter and not necessarily the views of AMN.</p>
<p>All comments that are not spam or wholly inappropriate are approved, we do not sort out opinions or points of view that are different from ours.</p>
</div><div class="vc_tta-container" data-vc-action="collapseAll"><div class="vc_general vc_tta vc_tta-accordion vc_tta-color-grey vc_tta-style-modern vc_tta-shape-square vc_tta-o-shape-group vc_tta-controls-align-left vc_tta-o-all-clickable"><div class="vc_tta-panels-container"><div class="vc_tta-panels"><div class="vc_tta-panel" id="1516307298313-0aa2500a-3d9d" data-vc-content=".vc_tta-panel-body"><div class="vc_tta-panel-heading"><h4 class="vc_tta-panel-title vc_tta-controls-icon-position-left"><a href="#1516307298313-0aa2500a-3d9d" data-vc-accordion="" data-vc-container=".vc_tta-container"><span class="vc_tta-title-text">Be Civil</span><i class="vc_tta-controls-icon vc_tta-controls-icon-plus"></i></a></h4></div><div class="vc_tta-panel-body">
	<div class="wpb_text_column wpb_content_element ">
		<div class="wpb_wrapper">
			<h2>This is a Civilized Place for Public Discussion</h2>
<p>Please treat this discussion with the same respect you would a public park. We, too, are a shared community resource  a place to share skills, knowledge and interests through ongoing conversation.</p>
<p>These are not hard and fast rules, merely guidelines to aid the human judgment of our community and keep this a clean and well-lighted place for civilized public discourse.</p>

		</div>
	</div>
</div></div><div class="vc_tta-panel" id="1516307298345-cd1a23f6-350e" data-vc-content=".vc_tta-panel-body"><div class="vc_tta-panel-heading"><h4 class="vc_tta-panel-title vc_tta-controls-icon-position-left"><a href="#1516307298345-cd1a23f6-350e" data-vc-accordion="" data-vc-container=".vc_tta-container"><span class="vc_tta-title-text">Make it better</span><i class="vc_tta-controls-icon vc_tta-controls-icon-plus"></i></a></h4></div><div class="vc_tta-panel-body">
	<div class="wpb_text_column wpb_content_element ">
		<div class="wpb_wrapper">
			<h2>Improve the Discussion</h2>
<p>Help us make this a great place for discussion by always working to improve the discussion in some way, however small. If you are not sure your post adds to the conversation, think over what you want to say and try again later.</p>
<p>The topics discussed here matter to us, and we want you to act as if they matter to you, too. Be respectful of the topics and the people discussing them, even if you disagree with some of what is being said.</p>

		</div>
	</div>
</div></div><div class="vc_tta-panel" id="1516307532810-95d881e2-6d73" data-vc-content=".vc_tta-panel-body"><div class="vc_tta-panel-heading"><h4 class="vc_tta-panel-title vc_tta-controls-icon-position-left"><a href="#1516307532810-95d881e2-6d73" data-vc-accordion="" data-vc-container=".vc_tta-container"><span class="vc_tta-title-text">Now the hard part!</span><i class="vc_tta-controls-icon vc_tta-controls-icon-plus"></i></a></h4></div><div class="vc_tta-panel-body">
	<div class="wpb_text_column wpb_content_element ">
		<div class="wpb_wrapper">
			<h2>Be Agreeable, Even When You Disagree</h2>
<p>You may wish to respond to something by disagreeing with it. Thats fine. But remember to&nbsp;<em>criticize ideas, not people</em>. Please avoid:</p>
<ul>
<li>Name-calling</li>
<li>Ad hominem attacks</li>
<li>Responding to a posts tone instead of its actual content</li>
<li>Knee-jerk contradiction</li>
</ul>
<p>Instead, provide reasoned counter-arguments that improve the conversation.</p>

		</div>
	</div>
</div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="wpb_column vc_column_container td-pb-span4"><div class="vc_column-inner "><div class="wpb_wrapper"></div></div></div></div>	</div>
